       </button>
       <h3>
        Driving directions
       </h3>
       <div class="tooltype-sub-title">
        MICHELIN recommended
       </div>
       <p>
        The route deemed to be the safest and simplest with minimal scope for error along the way. The default recommended route from Michelin.
       </p>
       <div class="tooltype-sub-title">
        Quickest
       </div>
       <p>
        The route likely to offer the shortest journey time to the chosen destination, favouring main roads and, in particular, highways.
       </p>
       <div class="tooltype-sub-title">
        Shortest
       </div>
       <p>
        The route offering the shortest distance to a destination via the most accessible roads. Journey times for this option will tend to be longer.
       </p>
       <div class="tooltype-sub-title">
        Discovery
       </div>
       <p>
        The route option for scenic roads that may have a touristic interest.
       </p>
       <div class="tooltype-sub-title">
        Economical
       </div>
       <p>
        The most fuel-efficient route that also avoids toll roads.
       </p>

    <div class="footer-item faq" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/FAQPage">
     <div itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
      <h2 class="footer-title" itemprop="name">
       Which services are offered by ViaMichelin ?
      </h2>
      <div class="footer-content" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
       <div itemprop="text">
        <p>
         ViaMichelin offers the following services:
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Maps">
           Online mapping
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          Multiple
          <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Routes">
           route calculation
          </a>
          options with the cost of the journey (fuel, tolls, vignettes)
         </li>
         <li>
          <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Traffic">
           Real-time road traffic info
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Hotels">
           Accommodation
          </a>
          and
          <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Search-Restaurants">
           restaurant reservations
          </a>
          for your journey and destination
         </li>
         <li>
          Highlighting
          <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Tourist-Attractions">
           tourist sites
          </a>
          to explore.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         In preparation or on the road, for everyday journeys and the holidays, ViaMichelin, through its expertise and know-how, accompanies you to offer peace of mind and the pleasure of discovery.
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
      <h2 class="footer-title" itemprop="name">
       Does ViaMichelin have a mobile application that provides access to road traffic information?
      </h2>
      <div class="footer-content" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
       <div itemprop="text">
        <p>
         ViaMichelin has a
         <strong>
          free mobile app
         </strong>
         . It is available as a free download for both Apple and Android. Find Michelin maps, routes and guidance with
         <strong>
          real-time traffic
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          GPS Navigation
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          3D maps
         </strong>
         with voice guidance and community alerts.
        </p>
        <p>
         Click
         <a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/viamichelin-gps-route-planner/id443142682">
          here
         </a>
         to download the Apple app
        </p>
        <p>
         Click
         <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.viamichelin.android.viamichelinmobile&amp;hl=en">
          here
         </a>
         to download the Android app
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
      <h2 class="footer-title" itemprop="name">
       Which type of routes can you calculate on ViaMichelin ?
      </h2>
      <div class="footer-content" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
       <div itemprop="text">
        <p>
         ViaMichelin offers
         <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Routes">
          route and distance calculations
         </a>
         between towns, addresses and points of interest for 4 possible modes of transport:
         <strong>
          car
         </strong>
         /
         <strong>
          motorcycle
         </strong>
         /
         <strong>
          bike
         </strong>
         /
         <strong>
          pedestrian
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         For car and motorcycle routes you can choose from the following variants:
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          <strong>
           Michelin recommended
          </strong>
          : this route option focuses on safety, simplicity and minimising any risk of route errors. This is the default route that Michelin recommends.
         </li>
         <li>
          <strong>
           The quickest
          </strong>
          (prioritising time): this route option takes the least time to reach the destination.
         </li>
         <li>
          <strong>
           The shortest
          </strong>
          (prioritising distance): this route option involves the shortest distance to reach the destination, whilst always remaining on passable roads.
         </li>
         <li>
          <strong>
           Discovery
          </strong>
          : this route option favours scenic routes of tourist interest.
         </li>
         <li>
          <strong>
           Economic
          </strong>
          : this route focuses on fuel efficiency and avoiding toll roads.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         You can add up to 6 stages to your route. These stages will also be included in the ViaMichelin GPS app if you have saved your route in your Michelin account.
        </p>
        <p>
         For every calculated route, ViaMichelin offers the choice of two or three itineraries and allows you to make an easy comparison.
        </p>
        <p>
         ViaMichelin can provide a
         <strong>
          detailed cost for your journey
         </strong>
         :
         <strong>
          fuel costs
         </strong>
         adapted to your vehicle and
         <strong>
          toll costs
         </strong>
         throughout Europe.
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
      <h2 class="footer-title" itemprop="name">
       Does ViaMichelin offer real-time traffic information?
      </h2>
      <div class="footer-content" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
       <div itemprop="text">
        <p>
         ViaMichelin provides
         <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Traffic">
          real-time traffic information
         </a>
         . To ensure you are well prepared for your trips, our site offers information on
         <strong>
          traffic jams, traffic accidents and roadworks
         </strong>
         , as well as
         <strong>
          slow moving traffic
         </strong>
         and
         <strong>
          weather conditions (snow, rain, ice)
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         The journey times provided in your route calculations take traffic conditions into account. The impact of traffic levels on your journey time is provided in the  Time  section of your route summary.
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
      <h2 class="footer-title" itemprop="name">
       Is it possible to book accommodation on ViaMichelin?
      </h2>
      <div class="footer-content" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
       <div itemprop="text">
        <p>
         ViaMichelin offers
         <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Hotels">
          accommodation booking
         </a>
         at no extra cost. In partnership with Booking, we offer a wide range of accommodation (hotels, gtes, B&amp;Bs, campsites, apartments) in your chosen location. You also have the option to read up on and
         <strong>
          book hotels selected from the MICHELIN Guide
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         The ViaMichelin advantage:
         <strong>
          choose a hotel along the route
         </strong>
         , or close to your destination, and access the
         <strong>
          Michelin hotel selections
         </strong>
         through a filter in the results list.
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
      <h2 class="footer-title" itemprop="name">
       Can you look up or book a restaurant on ViaMichelin ?
      </h2>
      <div class="footer-content" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
       <div itemprop="text">
        <p>
         ViaMichelin offers access to
         <strong>
          free information on
          <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Search-Restaurants">
           restaurants in the MICHELIN Guide
          </a>
         </strong>
         , anywhere in the world. A
         <strong>
          free online booking service
         </strong>
         is also available for participating restaurants. You can also make a booking with restaurants that are not featured in the MICHELIN Guide selection, for a restaurant stop along your journey or at your destination.
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
      <h2 class="footer-title" itemprop="name">
       What tourist information does ViaMichelin offer?
      </h2>
      <div class="footer-content" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
       <div itemprop="text">
        <p>
         ViaMichelin provides information on
         <a href="https://www.viamichelin.com/web/Tourist-Attractions">
          MICHELIN Green Guide tourist sites
         </a>
         around the world. You can find the list of
         <strong>
          Green Guide tourist sites
         </strong>
         as well as the rating for each site (1, 2 or 3 stars). You can also, of course,
         <strong>
          calculate the route to and from your chosen tourist site
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
